country_event = { 
	id = twrcroatia.1 #Intro
	title = twrcroatia.1.t
	desc = twrcroatia.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_croatia_intro

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = CRO_resistance_mechanic_enabled
		set_variable = {
			var = CRO_Resistance_level
			value = 25
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CRO_Military_Influence
			value = 30
		}
		set_country_flag = CRO_partisan_resistance_active
		set_country_flag = CRO_bosnian_resistance_active
		set_country_flag = CRO_chetnik_resistance_active

		1016 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_PARTISAN_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		103 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_PARTISAN_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		104 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_PARTISAN_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		109 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_USTASE_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		1030 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_USTASE_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		981 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_USTASE_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		982 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_USTASE_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
		983 = {
			set_state_flag = CRO_USTASE_CONTROLLED_STATE
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { 
		name = twrcroatia.1.a
	}
}

country_event = { # The Zagreb Uprising
	id = twrcroatia.2
	title = twrcroatia.2.t
	desc = twrcroatia.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_croatia_destroyed_church
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { 
		name = twrcroatia.2.a
		add_stability = -0.20
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Supreme Ustaša Council"
			desc = "USTASHA_COUNCIL_DESC"
			picture = "Ustasha_Council.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = ustasa_movement 
			traits = { cabinet_crisis }
		}
        add_ideas = CRO_HoG_Andrija_Artukovic 
        add_ideas = CRO_MoS_Jure_Francetic 
		custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_Chaos_in_Zagreb_tree_load_tt
		load_focus_tree = CRO_Bosnian_Uprising_Tree
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = twrnews.170 }
			clr_country_flag = CRO_Ante_Pavelic
			clr_country_flag = CRO_Andrija_Artukovic_SIC
			set_country_flag = CRO_NO_POGLAVNIK
			set_country_flag = CRO_NO_SIC
		}
	}
}

	desc = twrcroatia.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { 
		name = twrcroatia.3.a
                kill_ideology_leader = national_socialist
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Power Vacuum"
				#desc = ""
				#picture = ""
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_socialism
				traits = {
					#
				}
			}
                set_country_flag = Andrija_Artukovic_unavailable 
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			last_election = "1935.6.9"
			election_frequency = 12
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.51
		}
                add_ideas = {
                CRO_MoS_Ante_Vokic 
                CRO_FM_Vjekoslav_Vrancic 
                CRO_AM_Lovro_Susic 
                }
		load_focus_tree = CRO_HSS_Tree
		complete_national_focus = CRO_HSS_The_Peasants_Plot
	}
}

				}
			}
			40 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0

				}

		}
	}

country_event = { # Bosnia Declares Independence
	id = twrcroatia.19
	title = twrcroatia.19.t
	desc = twrcroatia.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bosnian_revolt
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			BOS = {
		        add_timed_idea = {
			        idea = BOS_For_Bosnia 
			        days = 175
		        }
                load_focus_tree = BOS_Uprising_Tree
                complete_national_focus = BOS_For_Bosnia
				transfer_state = 104
				transfer_state = 981
				transfer_state = 982
				load_oob = "BOS_REVOLT"
			}
			cro_remove_bosnia_modifiers = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_debug = yes
				}
				BOS = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Joker Omčo"
						desc = "Crazy_Hamburger_Desc"
						picture = "crazy_hamburger.dds"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = military_dictatorshipz
						traits = {
							#
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = twrcroatia.19.a
		load_focus_tree = CRO_Government_Revolt_Tree
		complete_national_focus = CRO_The_Revolt_Begins
		declare_war_on = {
			target = BOS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = croatiauprising.12
				days = 2
			}
			activate_mission = CRO_Bosnian_Ceasefire
			news_event = { id = twrnews.171 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Dreams of a Free Bosnia
	id = twrcroatia.36
	title = twrcroatia.36.t
	desc = twrcroatia.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bosnian_mountain
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Install a new leader
		name = twrcroatia.36.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_Homeguard_Increase_Influence_tt
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = COUNTRY_PATH_CRO_CONS
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { CRO_fash_support = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			cro_remove_bosnia_modifiers = yes
			104 = {
            	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bosnia_iv }
            }
			981 = {
            	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bosnia_iv }
            }
			982 = {
            	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bosnia_iv }
            }
		}
	}
	option = { # Free Autonomous Bosnia
		name = twrcroatia.36.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_HSS_Increase_Influence_tt
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = COUNTRY_PATH_CRO_PATAUT
					has_global_flag = COUNTRY_PATH_CRO_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { CRO_hss_support = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { 			
		cro_remove_bosnia_modifiers = yes
		}
		BOS = {
			transfer_state = 104
			transfer_state = 981
			transfer_state = 982
		CRO = {
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = BOS
				autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
			}
			else = {
			CRO = { puppet = BOS }
			}
		}
	}
			set_cosmetic_tag = BOS_Croatian_Autonomy 
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = conservative
					name = BOS_HSS_party
					long_name = BOS_HSS_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = BOS_HOS_party
					long_name = BOS_HOS_party_long
				}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = conservative
			last_election = "1935.6.9"
			election_frequency = 12
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservative

country_event = { # The Beginning of the Border War
	id = twrcroatia_borderwar.1
	title = twrcroatia_borderwar.1.t
	desc = twrcroatia_borderwar.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_domobran
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = twrcroatia_borderwar.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_HUN_border_war_begin_tt
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = {
				id = twrcroatia_borderwar.2
			}
		}
		CRO  = {
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = no
				attacker = {
					state = 819
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = twrcroatia_borderwar.3
					on_lose = twrcroatia_borderwar.4
					on_cancel = twrcroatia_borderwar.5
				}
							
				defender = {
					state = 45
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = twrcroatia_borderwar.6
					on_lose = twrcroatia_borderwar.7
					on_cancel = twrcroatia_borderwar.8
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = twrcroatia_borderwar.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = COUNTRY_PATH_CRO_CONS
					has_global_flag = COUNTRY_PATH_CRO_PATAUT
					has_global_flag = COUNTRY_PATH_CRO_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = CROAT_HUNGARIAN_WAR_ENDED
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = twrcroatia.231
	title = twrcroatia.231.t
	desc = twrcroatia.231.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_results
	
is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			var = CRO_Kosutic_support
			value = 40
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CRO_Kucar_support
			value = 35
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = CRO_Tripalo_support
			value = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { days = 15 id = cro_election_events.1 }
			country_event = { days = 10 id = cro_election_events.2 }
			country_event = { days = 5 id = cro_election_events.3 }
			set_popularities = {
				conservative = 40
				liberal = 35
				social_democrat = 25
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Kosutic
		name = twrcroatia.231.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 34
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = kosutic_selected_tt
		set_country_flag = kosutic_selected
	}
	
	option = { #Tripalo
		name = twrcroatia.231.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = tripalo_selected_tt
		set_country_flag = tripalo_selected
	}
	
	option = { #Kucar
		name = twrcroatia.231.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = kucar_selected_tt
		set_country_flag = kucar_selected
	}
}

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = croatiauprising.11.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_government = national_socialist
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = BOS
					}
					BOS = {

						exists = yes
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BOS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}


	picture = GFX_report_event_belgrade_ruins
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #We have won!
		name = croatiauprising.11.a
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.15
		hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas = CRO_Croatian_Civil_War_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CRO_has_won_against_the_uprising = yes
				
			}
			CRO_cw_cleanup = yes
		}
	}
}

					division = "name = \"1. Rezervna Legijska divizija'\" division_template = \"Crna Legija\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = ROOT
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"2. Rezervna Legijska divizija'\" division_template = \"Crna Legija\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = ROOT
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"3. Rezervna Legijska divizija'\" division_template = \"Crna Legija\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = ROOT
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"4. Rezervna Legijska divizija'\" division_template = \"Crna Legija\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = CRO_Francetic_Influence
				value = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = CRO_Artukovic_Loyalty
				value = 1
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = CRO_Artukovic_Influence
				value = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CRO_Lorkovic_DEAD
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = CRO_Lorkovic_Influence
					value = 5
				}
			}
			CRO_Ustase_Administration_influence_clamp = yes
		}
	}

country_event = { #Defeat in Bosnia
	id = croatiauprising.21
	title = croatiauprising.21.t
	desc = croatiauprising.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bosnian_revolt
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = bosnia_war_over_flag } 
	}
	immediate = { set_country_flag = lost_in_bosnia  set_country_flag = bosnia_war_over_flag }
	
	option = { #Damn them
		name = croatiauprising.21.a
		trigger = {
			is_fascist = yes
		}

		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CRO_Lorkovic_DEAD
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_grow_lorkovic_influence_high
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CRO_Artukovic_DEAD
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_reduce_artukovic_influence_high
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CRO_Francetic_DEAD
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CRO_reduce_francetic_loyalty_medium
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CRO_Artukovic_DEAD
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = CRO_Artukovic_Influence
					value = 15
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CRO_Francetic_DEAD
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = CRO_Francetic_Influence
					value = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CRO_Lorkovic_DEAD
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = CRO_Lorkovic_Influence
					value = 20
				}
			}
			CRO_Ustase_Administration_influence_clamp = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CRO_Lorkovic_DEAD
					}
				}
                kill_ideology_leader = national_socialist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Power Vacuum"
					#desc = ""
					#picture = ""
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = national_socialism
					traits = {
						#
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					last_election = "1935.6.9"
					election_frequency = 12
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.51
				}
                add_ideas = {
					CRO_HoG_Mladen_Lorkovic
					CRO_MoS_Ante_Vokic 
					CRO_FM_Vjekoslav_Vrancic 
					CRO_AM_Lovro_Susic 
                }
				load_focus_tree = CRO_HSS_Tree
				complete_national_focus = CRO_HSS_The_Peasants_Plot
				else = {
					country_event = {
						days = 2 id = croatiauprising.25
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Damn them
		name = croatiauprising.21.b
		trigger = {
			is_communist = yes
		}

		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -50
	}

				value = CRO_Artukovic_Influence

			}
		}

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { 
					has_id = 802
				}
				retire = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = CRO_Francetic_DEAD
			set_variable = {
				var = CRO_Francetic_Loyalty
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = CRO_Francetic_Influence
				value = 0
			}
			set_country_flag = Jure_Francetic_unavailable
		}
	}

		text = croatiamilitary.1.d

              }

		text = croatiamilitary.1.d
		trigger = { is_fascist = no }
              }

		}

country_event = { #Crusader revolt
	id = twr_croatia_crusader.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twr_croatia_crusader.2"}
	title = twr_croatia_crusader.2.t
	desc = twr_croatia_crusader.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ustaska_vojnica

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CRO
				}
				add_core_of = HER
				}
				HER = {
				transfer_state = 983
				IF = {
				limit = {
					BOS = { exists = yes }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BOS
					type = annex_everything
						}
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Križari"		
						division_names_group = CRO_CRU_01
					
						regiments = {
						mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						}
						support = {
						}
					}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"1. Križarska Divizija'\" division_template = \"Križari\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = HER
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"2. Križarska Divizija'\" division_template = \"Križari\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = HER
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"3.  Križarska divizija'\" division_template = \"Križari\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = HER
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"4.  Križarska divizija'\" division_template = \"Križari\" start_experience_factor = 0.3" owner = HER
							}
						}					
					}
				}
			}
	
	option = {

				declare_war_on = {
					target = HER
					type = annex_everything
					}

					target = HER
					type = annex_everything
					}
        	HER = { change_tag_from = CRO }
		}
	}
